5276 | |sokanon| | `[it pours], it rains' | II | Trumbull 1903 | \lx |sokanon|
\ps II

\sn 1
\ge `[it pours], it rains'
\so Mt.7.25

\xv Onk woh kittinnumauúnnumw∞ sokanon kutohkeyeuwóut, uttoh adt tapeneunkquok, negonne sokanon, kah maumachish sokanunk,...
\xe Tha
5278 | |uspunauónat|, |ushpun-|, |aspun-|, |ashpun-|, |spun-|, |ushpunát|, etc. | `to happen unexpectedly, to chance'; +`to befall sb, unto sb' | AI+"O", long-vowel stem; the relative root initial ("so") may be cataphoric to nominal expressions, giving the verb the appearance of taking an object. | Trumbull 1903 | \lx |uspunauónat|, |ushpun-|, |aspun-|, |ashpun-|, |spun-|, |ushpunát|, etc.

8913 | |-w'| |  |  | \lx |-w'|
\nt Linguist's Remark: The inseparable pronoun of the 3d pers. sing. and pl. Before |w| it coalesces with that letter, and the sound of |∞| is substituted. Before a vowel |'t| or |ut| is inserted for euphony, as |ohtomp| `a bow', |wutohtomp| `his bow'.

9653 | |wuttaihe| | `his, (is) his, belongs to him' | NA, NI? - category and form (with elusive |h|'s) uncertain, though there are AI verb forms in this entry, belonging to a verb of possession. The form |wuttaihe| appears to be used attributively as well as predicatively. It is presumably a dependent noun, perhaps to a stem of shape |-aih-e-|. | \lx |wuttaihe|
\nt +Linguist's Remark: Requires further study and reorganization
\ps NA, NI? - category and form (with elusive |h|'s) uncertain, though there are AI verb forms in this entry, belonging to a verb of possession. The form |wuttaihe| appears to be used attributively as well as predicatively. It is presumably a dependent noun, perhaps to a stem of shape |-aih-e-|.
